## Call stats

<details>
<summary> Inlined calls and frame stats </summary>


This shows what fraction of calls to Python functions are inlined (i.e.
not having a call at the C level) and for those that are not, where the
call comes from.  The various categories overlap.

Also includes the count of frame objects created.

<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left"></th>
<th align="right">Count</th>
<th align="right">Ratio</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls to PyEval_EvalDefault</td>
<td align="right">2,272,126,375</td>
<td align="right">27.0%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls to Python functions inlined</td>
<td align="right">6,149,776,909</td>
<td align="right">73.0%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (total)</td>
<td align="right">2,272,126,375</td>
<td align="right">27.0%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (vector)</td>
<td align="right">1,420,196,872</td>
<td align="right">16.9%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (generator)</td>
<td align="right">851,929,503</td>
<td align="right">10.1%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (legacy)</td>
<td align="right">4,417,752</td>
<td align="right">0.1%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (function vectorcall)</td>
<td align="right">1,415,750,171</td>
<td align="right">16.8%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">Calls via PyEval_EvalFrame (build class)</td>
<td align="right">28,949</td>
<td align="right">0.0%</td>
